\hypertarget{interfaceMathLogSpace__mod_1_1getLogSpace}{}\doxysection{Math\+Log\+Space\+\_\+mod\+::get\+Log\+Space Interface Reference}
\label{interfaceMathLogSpace__mod_1_1getLogSpace}\index{MathLogSpace\_mod::getLogSpace@{MathLogSpace\_mod::getLogSpace}}


Return the {\ttfamily Log\+Space} output argument with {\ttfamily size(\+Log\+Space)} elements of logarithmically-\/evenly-\/spaced values over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}base$\ast$$\ast$logx1, base$\ast$$\ast$logx2\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily logx1 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} logx2}, or over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}logx2, logx1\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily logx2 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} logx1}.  




\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
Return the {\ttfamily Log\+Space} output argument with {\ttfamily size(\+Log\+Space)} elements of logarithmically-\/evenly-\/spaced values over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}base$\ast$$\ast$logx1, base$\ast$$\ast$logx2\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily logx1 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} logx2}, or over the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}logx2, logx1\mbox{]}} if {\ttfamily logx2 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} logx1}. 


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em Log\+Space} & \+: The output contiguous array of shape {\ttfamily (\+:)} of type either {\ttfamily real} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aaf5c6c840ed0befe5a37da626c35716f}{RK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a855643f887b4c787e6542e9e7849680f}{RK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aeef7c44b90b75aeeebdef1da504886cb}{RK128}} or {\ttfamily complex} of kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ac8b456bd9511bc9a52b4a03bda4b72df}{CK32}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_aa6ea61256fca0b20db0ec2b90755b9f3}{CK64}}, or \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_ad3873e1ecc5eb3cf3651f72630cae087}{CK128}} containing the log-\/evenly-\/spaced sequence within the interval specified by {\ttfamily logx1} and {\ttfamily logx2}. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em logx1} & \+: The input scalar of the same type and kind as {\ttfamily Log\+Space} representing the starting exponent such that {\ttfamily base$\ast$$\ast$logx1} is the starting value of the sequence. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em logx2} & \+: The input scalar of the same type and kind as {\ttfamily Log\+Space} representing the ending exponent such that {\ttfamily base$\ast$$\ast$logx1} is the last value of the sequence. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em fopen} & \+: The input scalar of type {\ttfamily logical} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a68ac316f10b57be996670bc7c0abed9d}{LK}}. If {\ttfamily .true.}, the {\ttfamily Log\+Space} will be {\bfseries{f}}irst-\/open, meaning that {\ttfamily logx1} will NOT be in the output {\ttfamily Log\+Space} sequence ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily .false.}). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em lopen} & \+: The input scalar of type {\ttfamily logical} of default kind \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceConstants__mod_a68ac316f10b57be996670bc7c0abed9d}{LK}}. If {\ttfamily .true.}, the {\ttfamily Log\+Space} will be {\bfseries{l}}ast-\/open, meaning that {\ttfamily logx2} will NOT be in the output {\ttfamily Log\+Space} sequence ({\bfseries{optional}}, default = {\ttfamily .false.}). \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em base} & \+: The input scalar of type {\ttfamily real} but the same kind as {\ttfamily Log\+Space} representing the the base of the logarithm ({\bfseries{oprional}}, default = {\ttfamily exp(1)}, that is, Euler\`{}s number).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This procedure is {\ttfamily pure}.

Setting both {\ttfamily fopen = .true.} and {\ttfamily lopen = .true.} will lead to an output Log\+Space whose points are centers of the {\ttfamily count + 1} equally-\/sized bins in the interval {\ttfamily \mbox{[}logx1,logx2\mbox{]}}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
